                            etype 0x8864
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 866 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8864/PPPoE Session/Multicast"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            dst-mac 01:00:5e:00:00:00 ff:ff:ff:80:00:00
                            etype 0x8864
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 899 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8864/PPPoE Session/Others"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            etype 0x8864
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 933 create
                        action accept
                        description "Others/Others/Broadcast"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            dst-mac ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 966 create
                        action accept
                        description "Others/Others/Multicast"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            dst-mac 01:00:5e:00:00:00 ff:ff:ff:80:00:00
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 999 create
                        action accept
                        description "Others/Others/Others"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                        exit
                    exit
                    no shutdown
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit
